<Review>The selection of beverages at Little Sweet is huge! Fruit, milk, blends. They have them all here!
I like the fact that there is an ordering stand outside the doorway. Then when your drink comes up the staff call your name.
You can scan the QR code on the window to see the menu.
You can also order snacks.
Convenient for visiting Golden Gate Park and the food corridors of 9th Avenue & Irving Streets (the Inner Sunset).
I would spend a substantial amount of $ on Little Sweets drinks if I lived closer...good thing I don‚Äôt!<//Review>< Date>

The mango pomelo sago is so delicious here! Their waffle pastries are also so good too. My friends and I came here for an afternoon snack and this hit the spot. It's a bit pricey for $8 but the cups are cute.

I came here and they have a QR code for you to order online. It was super easy to order. Then you get a text to pick up your order. And my order was done 10 min faster than they said it was!

Little sweet is so good and super easy to order. There were a lot of people waiting outside and social distancing safely for their orders. I would absolutely recommend this place to friends and fellow boba lovers!</Review>

< review>
Black sugar fresh milk with small boba is the best one we have ever had! We have kids and we always look for a fresh milk (non-caffeinated) drink and they have mastered that. We have tried that same drink elsewhere and no one can replicate this masterpiece at the Little Sweet. You can control the sweetness level and the dairy. You can also request more boba! It's warm fresh boba mixed with fresh cold milk. It's a delicious treat!< /review>

< Review>
After leaving the restaurant Los Balcones because of their incompetence to serve customers, I was pleasantly surprised to find The Parker Room literally right next door. I've had this gem bookmarked for a while so it was a special treat.. the only thing is that The Parker Room is connected to the Los Balcones barf (read previous review to comprehend my negative feelings). It looks closed from the outside but don't let their darn good tinted doors fool ya. Once you enter, your first reaction is going to be "I feel claustrophobic" because it's tiny and cramped if you come on a busy night. It's an informal friendly atmosphere with great happy hour deals and cocktails. There's a wide selection of finger food, main entrees, and alcoholic beverages for HH from 6-8 PM (I believe every day of the week). And I'm talking about $7 food items and well drinks!! What a steal! All our food items exceeded our expectations and was pleasantly enjoyable. The bartenders/waitresses were super friendly and were able to run the whole place with just two of em'. I feel in love with everyone's aura and to top it off they played great jazz music. From what I know, they have live jazz performance on Tuesday's.

Don't bring a group of people because everyone will not fit. For a low key one on one time, perfect. Enjoy some good food, while sipping on a cocktail and listening to great music! *In Arnold Schwarzenegger's voice* I'll be back.< /Review>

<time>1568951105753< /time><rating>5</rating><text>I have been seeing Dr. Park and now Dr. Kang at Glendale Dermatology for the past couple of years, and couldn't be happier with their service, results, time spent with me at each session, detailed explanation of process and costs, and their results!  I have loved them so much, I've referred several clients of my own from ElectroYogi for their dermatological concerns, and my clients have all been thrilled, too!

Dr. Kang has been my doctor recently, as Dr. Park moved to the West Hills location, I believe.  Dr. Kang has helped me with some skin growths/raised small moles and such, where she zaps them off the skin with overnight healing time.  As a woman in my mid/late 40s, I've also been recently inquiring about the different cosmetic procedures offered at the office.  Dr. Kang always explains exactly how things would work, what they would cost, any side effects or downtime, and more. She is terrific also because she has not once pushed me into any treatments. In fact, twice I went to ask her more details about what I could do for the lines above my upper lip, which are really the only thing about my aging face that frustrates me, and each time she carefully walked me through what the process would be , and never once encouraged me to 'go for it.'

That said, just today, after more than a year of consideration, I did my first ever cosmetic procedure for those upper lip lines.  We did a combination of Volbella dermal filler and a tiny amount of botox to help with the staying power of the line filler.  The process was fascinating, and looks so far great.  I have a small amount of swelling above my upper lip, but it is already going down, and I am happy with the immediate reduction of the lines. She did not plump up my upper and lower lip at all, and really focused on helping me with the lines while keeping a super natural look. Dr. Kang informed me that my naturally (and as a child, embarrassingly) big lips have lost some volume at my age, but she didn't try to have me fill the actual lips to be any bigger.  I'm looking forward to seeing how it looks in a couple of days.

<Rate>4<//Rate>< Review>
A nice place for a nerf gun battle. A nice size for larger parties but the obstacles in their play area is a bit sparse. You have 75 minutes of play which has a good amount of time but it's mostly free play. There was one game between teams with scoring and that was really fun. A bit more "organized" play would have been nice but the kids didn't seem to mind.

Although you can upgrade the party for $4/child so they can try out a larger variety of guns I would recommend you stay basic. The larger guns tend to jam more and take longer to load.

You can bring in water and a fruit plate platter but food and drinks for a party needs to be ordered thru the venue.</Review>

<Rate>5</Rate><Pics>None</Pics><Text>My Star Scale:
1 Star = Do not recommend
2 Star = Do not recommend but there were      positive aspects of the experience.
3 Star = Would recommend
4 Star = Would recommend ++service OR ++ food OR ++ ambiance (2 of 3)
5 Star = Would recommend ++service AND ++ food AND ++ambiance (3 of 3)

So the new Mastro's in SF is all about the hype and they definitely come though. Rediculous ambiance and service to back up the food, you are definitely getting your money's worth at this awesome high end steak and seafood restaurant. I've been to other Mastro's locations and this one ranks highly amongst the chain.  The attention to detail and food execution was impressive. Gluten free items are in abundance here and since they serve a la carte, ordering gluten free couldn't be easier!  By design, appetizers and side dishes are meant to be served family style. We went with lobster mashed potatoes, brussel sprouts, and steamed spinach. All awesome choices and very complementary to the main dishes we all chose.   Mastro's is known for their steaks right?  So I ordered up a Kansas City strip (basically a bone in NY strip). Bone in, changed the entire flavor profile of the strip for me and took it to an entirely different level. They asked how I would like it cooked and they hit it exactly as I asked for, medium with red in the center (a true medium).  Mastro's also serves A5 wagyu at up to $300 bucks a cut, but I know what I can appreciate and the strip I ordered was absolutely delicious.  We didn't order seafood during this visit but I've had the signature seafood tower here before and if you are up for awesome chilled lobster, crab, oysters, shrimp etc, this is a must have.  We corked our our own wine but the wine selection is never ending here, and they have a great selection at various price points to fit what you are looking for. Very attentive wait service but not overwhelming at the same time.  5 Star for sure.  If your are looking for high end quality food, awesome service and fantastic ambiance then this is the spot to go to. You don't just stumble across Mastro's SF, you plan on going there....<//Text>< username>
Amit Pall< /username>

I will highly recommend this place to anyone looking for a really nice upscale dinner without getting a coursed meal.
There is a strict upscale dress code.
Making reservations its ez by phone or online.
The cork fee is 40 dollars for a 750mil bottle.
We opted to bring our bottle of Dom perignon witch if purchased on side will run you for $300
So I payed $170 for my bottle plus $40 cork fee and saved me a few  bucks.
Prices are to be expected high, and average tap for 2 with a few cocktails a few appetisers 2 antrees and dessert will run at about  $300+.
We had 2 appetisers, 2 cocktails, 2 antrees, 2 side dishes and a dessert.
Our bill was 375$
Here is a list of dishes ordered.
Roasted bone marrow.
Seafood tower.
South of France cocktail.
Elder flower martini.
Filet 8oz.
Bone-In Filet 12oz.
Alaskan King Crab Black Truffle Gnocchi.
Rosemary Garlic SauteÃÅed Mushrooms.
Butter Cake.
The Bone marrow is really good an will recomend it to anyone willing to try something new. How ever the one we got was a bit gamey. I have to say I had better but I would still recommend it.
please note that the seafood tower is fully customisable and they will plated on a tower with dri ice on it witch make it really cool and hazy I recommend if your trying to impress your special someone or if you just love sea food we got shrimp cocktail which is 3 jumbo size shrimp they are extremely fresh and succulent also got 2 king crab claws that I would not recommend getting due to their small size your better of getting the king crab legs.
The 2 cocktail we got were really good and would recommend trying them out.
The filets were good but I wish I actually had ordered the Bone in ribeye.
The side dishes were delicious and huge they come on a big hot saute pan which completely kill the hole upscale dinner experience in my opinion.
I mean here we are sitting with this really nice dinner on a beautiful set table and the they bring out two big saut√© pans and leave them there on the middle on the table personally I would recommend the sides to be plated on a nice side dish patle or some kind of small cast iron plate but that's just me.
Over all our experience here was amazing and the food was great along with really nice and friendly staff and professionall service.< /Text>

<user_name>Anil Chokshi<//user_name><date>1578422897300</date><Rate>1</Rate><Text>If you‚Äôre looking for a fantastic steakhouse with quality steak, amazing service, great ambience and satisfaction for the premium price, KEEP LOOKING.... Most overrated restaurant and dining experience in SF. I had high hopes for Mastro‚Äôs. They have some serious kinks to work out in this restaurant. I have never waited so long (nearly an hour) for a table when a reservation was booked in advance. It took 30 minutes to get drinks after we put our order in at the bar while waiting. By the time we got seated and our orders came, we literally spent 3.5 hours in this place and we were only 2 people. And the most peculiar thing is apparently the VIP bread basket is the most exclusive item on their menu. It literally took 30 minutes before we finally got a bread basket, despite my multiple check-ins.

Management has not spent enough time educating their staff on the menu or the wine list.

The ambience was almost like walking into the set of a ghetto music video. Why is the music so loud and obnoxious? Why does the decor look like a high end brothel? For such an expensive restaurant, this place has ZERO CLASS and poor ambiance.

The only positives here were our table server had a lovely personality. Unfortunately, poor management and operational inefficiencies make her job very hard.

Food wise, I don‚Äôt find the product worth the price. I ordered a fillet medium rare. It was ok at best. It was dry, had no tenderness, and was over-salted. The Brussel sprouts tasted like the grass growing in my backyard with some salt poured over it. There was so much cream in the mashed potatoes, I thought I had drank an entire gravy boat after two bites.

Drink wise, if you‚Äôre going to charge $20+ for a cocktail on the rocks, use a single clear ice cube. That is standard at most cocktail bars when ordering an old fashioned or similar cocktail. Mastro‚Äôs used the same ice in the cocktails as their water glasses.

Additionally, the design is poorly done. For a massive two story restaurant, there should be a bathroom available on each level. Also, at this price point there should be valet parking.

Every steakhouse in SF is better than this one, including your own house with a cut of grocery chain store meat on the grill.

Save your time and  money. Go elsewhere.< /Text>< Pics>
